--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_F-150/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_F-150/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD F-150 → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_F-150/Config/TDPatterns/LeftRight.lua ---

--[[
    LeftRight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD F-150 → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M7(1)
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.3);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1);
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2);
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3);
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4);
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5);
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6);
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7);
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8);
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9);
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10);
	local S1 = elsModule(ELSModel.S1);
	local S2 = elsModule(ELSModel.S2);
	local S3 = elsModule(ELSModel.S3);
	local S4 = elsModule(ELSModel.S4);
	local Q1 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q1);
	local Q2 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q2);
	local Q3 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q3);
	local Q4 = elsModule(ELSModel.Q4);
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1);
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2);
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local W1 = elsModule(ELSModel.W1);
	local W2 = elsModule(ELSModel.W2);
	local W3 = elsModule(ELSModel.W3);
	local W4 = elsModule(ELSModel.W4);	

	if enabled then
		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				T1(1)
				T2(1)
				T3(1)
				T4(1)
				T5(1)
				T6(1)				
				T7(1)
				T8(1)
				T9(1)
				T10(1)				
				wait(0.03)	
			end
		end)

		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				F1(1)
				F2(1)
				wait(0.065)							
			end
		end)		
		task.defer(function()
			while true do				
				S1(0, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				S2(0, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				S3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				S4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				wait(0.12)

				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.135)					

				S1(0)
				S2(0)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.12)						

				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.135)					

				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(0)
				S4(0)
				wait(0.12)						

				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.135)		

				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(0)
				S4(0)
				wait(0.12)						

				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.135)						
			end
		end)		

		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				Q1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				Q2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				Q3(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				Q4(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));

				Q1(1)

				wait(0.065)						

				Q1(1)

				wait(0.13)					

				Q1(1)
				Q2(1)
				Q3(1)
				Q4(1)
				wait(0.065)					
			end
		end)		

		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				R1(1)
				R2(0)
				R3(1)
				R4(0)
				wait(0.12)	

				R1(1)
				R2(1)
				R3(1)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.055)					

				R1(1)
				R2(0)
				R3(1)
				R4(0)
				wait(0.12)	

				R1(1)
				R2(1)
				R3(1)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.055)		

				R1(1)
				R2(0)
				R3(1)
				R4(0)
				wait(0.12)	

				R1(1)
				R2(1)
				R3(1)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.055)		

				R1(0)
				R2(1)
				R3(0)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.12)	

				R1(1)
				R2(1)
				R3(1)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.055)		

				R1(0)
				R2(1)
				R3(0)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.12)	

				R1(1)
				R2(1)
				R3(1)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.055)		

				R1(0)
				R2(1)
				R3(0)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.12)	

				R1(1)
				R2(1)
				R3(1)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.055)		

			end
		end)	

		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				W1(1)
				W2(0)
				W3(1)
				W4(0)
				wait(0.085)	

				W1(1)
				W2(1)
				W3(1)
				W4(1)
				wait(0.055)					

				W1(1)
				W2(0)
				W3(1)
				W4(0)
				wait(0.085)	

				W1(1)
				W2(1)
				W3(1)
				W4(1)
				wait(0.055)			

				W1(0)

				W4(1)

				wait(0.055)			

				W1(0)

				W3(0)
				W4(1)
				wait(0.085)	

				W1(1)
				W2(1)
				W3(1)
				W4(1)
				wait(0.055)	
			end
		end)	
	else
		T1(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		T2(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		T5(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		T6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T9(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T10(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		Q1(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		Q2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		Q3(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		Q4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));			
		S1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		S2(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		S3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		S4(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		F1(1)
		F2(1)		
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)	
		W1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		W2(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		W3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		W4(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));			
	end
end

	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9);

	local S1 = elsModule(ELSModel.S1);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

		end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Unmarked_Taurus/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Unmarked Taurus → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

					F7(1);
					F8(0);
					F9(1);
					F10(0);
					wait(0.06)

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					F5(1);
					F6(1);
					F7(1);
					F8(1);
					F9(1);
					F10(1);
					wait(0.07)
				end
			end)
		end)()			

	else
		F1(1);
		F2(1);
		F3(1);
		F4(1);
		F5(1);
		F6(1);
		F7(1);
		F8(1);
		F9(1);
		F10(1);	
	end
end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Bearcat/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Bearcat → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Bearcat/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Bearcat → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Bearcat/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Bearcat → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i,v in next, body.Headlights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name == 'Orange' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
			end
		end
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i,v in next, body.Headlights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name == 'Orange' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			end
		end
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Bearcat/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Bearcat → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Bearcat/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Bearcat → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

    Parent: TDPatterns

]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-150/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)

	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2) 
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);					
				wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				T5(1);
				T6(1);
				T7(1);
				T8(1);		
				wait()	
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					R5(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R6(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));						
					wait(0.15)						

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		

					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		
				end
			end)
		end)()		
				
		
	else
		T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
		T5(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T6(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));						
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		R5(1)
		R6(1)
		R7(1)
		R8(1)		
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350_Closed_back/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 Closed back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350_Closed_back/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 Closed back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350_Closed_back/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 Closed back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350_Closed_back/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 Closed back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350_Open_back/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 Open back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350_Open_back/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 Open back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350_Open_back/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 Open back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_F-350_Open_back/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT F-350 Open back → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/VPD_ERT/VPD_ERT_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → VPD:ERT → VPD:ERT Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:49
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Divisions/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/POU/Tools/Notepad/LocalScript.client.lua ---

--[[
    LocalScript (LocalScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Divisions → British Columbia Sheriff Service → POU → Tools → Notepad
    Parent: Notepad
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:34
]]
bin = script.Parent  
char = nil

function onButton1Down(mouse) 
	local Anim = script.Parent.RadioUse
	local AnimTrack = script.Parent.Parent.Humanoid:LoadAnimation(Anim)	
local plr = game:GetService('Players'):getPlayerFromCharacter(char)
if plr ~= nil then
local plrgui = plr:findFirstChild("PlayerGui")
if plrgui ~= nil then
local find = plrgui:findFirstChild("DeathNote" .. " - " .. plr.Name)
if find == nil then
local new = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
new.Name = "DeathNote" .. " - " .. plr.Name
new.Parent = plrgui
local deathnote = script:findFirstChild("Notebook")
if deathnote ~= nil then
deathnote.Parent = new
end
AnimTrack:Play()
end
end
end
end

function onDeselected() 
	local plr = game:GetService('Players'):getPlayerFromCharacter(char)
if plr ~= nil then
local plrgui = plr:findFirstChild("PlayerGui")
if plrgui ~= nil then
local find = plrgui:findFirstChild("DeathNote" .. " - " .. plr.Name)
if find ~= nil then
local ntbk = find:findFirstChild("Notebook")
if ntbk ~= nil then
ntbk.Parent = script
find.Parent = nil
end
end
end
end
	for _,anim in pairs(char.Humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
		if anim.Name == "RadioUse" then
		 anim:Stop()
end
end
end

function onSelected(mouse)
char = script.Parent.Parent
local user = script:findFirstChild("Notebook"):findFirstChild("User")
user.Value = game:GetService('Players'):getPlayerFromCharacter(char).Name
mouse.Icon = ""
mouse.Button1Down:connect(function() onButton1Down(mouse) end)
end

bin.Equipped:connect(onSelected)
bin.Unequipped:connect(onDeselected)

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Divisions/British_Columbia_Sheriff_Service/POU/Tools/POU_Badge/qPerfectionWeld.server.lua ---

--[[
    qPerfectionWeld (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Divisions → British Columbia Sheriff Service → POU → Tools → POU Badge
    Parent: POU Badge
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:34
]]
-- Created by Quenty (@Quenty, follow me on twitter).
-- Should work with only ONE copy, seamlessly with weapons, trains, et cetera.
-- Parts should be ANCHORED before use. It will, however, store relatives values and so when tools are reparented, it'll fix them.

--[[ INSTRUCTIONS
- Place in the model
- Make sure model is anchored
- That's it. It will weld the model and all children. 

THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 

This script is designed to be used is a regular script. In a local script it will weld, but it will not attempt to handle ancestory changes. 
]]

--[[ DOCUMENTATION
- Will work in tools. If ran more than once it will not create more than one weld.  This is especially useful for tools that are dropped and then picked up again.
- Will work in PBS servers
- Will work as long as it starts out with the part anchored
- Stores the relative CFrame as a CFrame value
- Takes careful measure to reduce lag by not having a joint set off or affected by the parts offset from origin
- Utilizes a recursive algorith to find all parts in the model
- Will reweld on script reparent if the script is initially parented to a tool.
- Welds as fast as possible
]]

-- qPerfectionWeld.lua
-- Created 10/6/2014
-- Author: Quenty
-- Version 1.0.3

-- Updated 10/14/2014 - Updated to 1.0.1
--- Bug fix with existing ROBLOX welds ? Repro by asimo3089

-- Updated 10/14/2014 - Updated to 1.0.2
--- Fixed bug fix. 

-- Updated 10/14/2014 - Updated to 1.0.3
--- Now handles joints semi-acceptably. May be rather hacky with some joints. :/

local NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS = false -- If you set this to true it will never break joints (this can create some welding issues, but can save stuff like hinges).


local function CallOnChildren(Instance, FunctionToCall)
	-- Calls a function on each of the children of a certain object, using recursion.  

	FunctionToCall(Instance)

	for _, Child in next, Instance:GetChildren() do
		CallOnChildren(Child, FunctionToCall)
	end
end

local function GetNearestParent(Instance, ClassName)
	-- Returns the nearest parent of a certain class, or returns nil

	local Ancestor = Instance
	repeat
		Ancestor = Ancestor.Parent
		if Ancestor == nil then
			return nil
		end
	until Ancestor:IsA(ClassName)

	return Ancestor
end

local function GetBricks(StartInstance)
	local List = {}

	-- if StartInstance:IsA("BasePart") then
	-- 	List[#List+1] = StartInstance
	-- end

	CallOnChildren(StartInstance, function(Item)
		if Item:IsA("BasePart") then
			List[#List+1] = Item;
		end
	end)

	return List
end

local function Modify(Instance, Values)
	-- Modifies an Instance by using a table.  

	assert(type(Values) == "table", "Values is not a table");

	for Index, Value in next, Values do
		if type(Index) == "number" then
			Value.Parent = Instance
		else
			Instance[Index] = Value
		end
	end
	return Instance
end

local function Make(ClassType, Properties)
	-- Using a syntax hack to create a nice way to Make new items.  

	return Modify(Instance.new(ClassType), Properties)
end

local Surfaces = {"TopSurface", "BottomSurface", "LeftSurface", "RightSurface", "FrontSurface", "BackSurface"}
local HingSurfaces = {"Hinge", "Motor", "SteppingMotor"}

local function HasWheelJoint(Part)
	for _, SurfaceName in pairs(Surfaces) do
		for _, HingSurfaceName in pairs(HingSurfaces) do
			if Part[SurfaceName].Name == HingSurfaceName then
				return true
			end
		end
	end
	
	return false
end

local function ShouldBreakJoints(Part)
	--- We do not want to break joints of wheels/hinges. This takes the utmost care to not do this. There are
	--  definitely some edge cases. 

	if NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS then
		return false
	end
	
	if HasWheelJoint(Part) then
		return false
	end
	
	local Connected = Part:GetConnectedParts()
	
	if #Connected == 1 then
		return false
	end
	
	for _, Item in pairs(Connected) do
		if HasWheelJoint(Item) then
			return false
		elseif not Item:IsDescendantOf(script.Parent) then
			return false
		end
	end
	
	return true
end

local function WeldTogether(Part0, Part1, JointType, WeldParent)
	--- Weld's 2 parts together
	-- @param Part0 The first part
	-- @param Part1 The second part (Dependent part most of the time).
	-- @param [JointType] The type of joint. Defaults to weld.
	-- @param [WeldParent] Parent of the weld, Defaults to Part0 (so GC is better).
	-- @return The weld created.

	JointType = JointType or "Weld"
	local RelativeValue = Part1:FindFirstChild("qRelativeCFrameWeldValue")
	
	local NewWeld = Part1:FindFirstChild("qCFrameWeldThingy") or Instance.new(JointType)
	Modify(NewWeld, {
		Name = "qCFrameWeldThingy";
		Part0  = Part0;
		Part1  = Part1;
		C0     = CFrame.new();--Part0.CFrame:inverse();
		C1     = RelativeValue and RelativeValue.Value or Part1.CFrame:toObjectSpace(Part0.CFrame); --Part1.CFrame:inverse() * Part0.CFrame;-- Part1.CFrame:inverse();
		Parent = Part1;
	})

	if not RelativeValue then
		RelativeValue = Make("CFrameValue", {
			Parent     = Part1;
			Name       = "qRelativeCFrameWeldValue";
			Archivable = true;
			Value      = NewWeld.C1;
		})
	end

	return NewWeld
end

local function WeldParts(Parts, MainPart, JointType, DoNotUnanchor)
	-- @param Parts The Parts to weld. Should be anchored to prevent really horrible results.
	-- @param MainPart The part to weld the model to (can be in the model).
	-- @param [JointType] The type of joint. Defaults to weld. 
	-- @parm DoNotUnanchor Boolean, if true, will not unachor the model after cmopletion.
	
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if ShouldBreakJoints(Part) then
			Part:BreakJoints()
		end
	end
	
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if Part ~= MainPart then
			WeldTogether(MainPart, Part, JointType, MainPart)
		end
	end

	if not DoNotUnanchor then
		for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
			Part.Anchored = false
		end
		MainPart.Anchored = false
	end
end

local function PerfectionWeld()	
	local Tool = GetNearestParent(script, "Tool")

	local Parts = GetBricks(script.Parent)
	local PrimaryPart = Tool and Tool:FindFirstChild("Handle") and Tool.Handle:IsA("BasePart") and Tool.Handle or script.Parent:IsA("Model") and script.Parent.PrimaryPart or Parts[1]

	if PrimaryPart then
		WeldParts(Parts, PrimaryPart, "Weld", false)
	else
		warn("qWeld - Unable to weld part")
	end
	
	return Tool
end

local Tool = PerfectionWeld()


if Tool and script.ClassName == "Script" then
	--- Don't bother with local scripts

	script.Parent.AncestryChanged:connect(function()
		PerfectionWeld()
	end)
end

--[[
    qPerfectionWeld (Script)

    Parent: DND ID
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:34

-- Created by Quenty (@Quenty, follow me on twitter).
-- Should work with only ONE copy, seamlessly with weapons, trains, et cetera.
-- Parts should be ANCHORED before use. It will, however, store relatives values and so when tools are reparented, it'll fix them.

--[[ INSTRUCTIONS
- Place in the model
- Make sure model is anchored
- That's it. It will weld the model and all children. 

THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 
THIS SCRIPT SHOULD BE USED ONLY BY ITSELF. THE MODEL SHOULD BE ANCHORED. 

This script is designed to be used is a regular script. In a local script it will weld, but it will not attempt to handle ancestory changes. 
]]

--[[ DOCUMENTATION
- Will work in tools. If ran more than once it will not create more than one weld.  This is especially useful for tools that are dropped and then picked up again.
- Will work in PBS servers
- Will work as long as it starts out with the part anchored
- Stores the relative CFrame as a CFrame value
- Takes careful measure to reduce lag by not having a joint set off or affected by the parts offset from origin
- Utilizes a recursive algorith to find all parts in the model
- Will reweld on script reparent if the script is initially parented to a tool.
- Welds as fast as possible
]]

-- qPerfectionWeld.lua
-- Created 10/6/2014
-- Author: Quenty
-- Version 1.0.3

-- Updated 10/14/2014 - Updated to 1.0.1
--- Bug fix with existing ROBLOX welds ? Repro by asimo3089

-- Updated 10/14/2014 - Updated to 1.0.2
--- Fixed bug fix. 

-- Updated 10/14/2014 - Updated to 1.0.3
--- Now handles joints semi-acceptably. May be rather hacky with some joints. :/

local NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS = false -- If you set this to true it will never break joints (this can create some welding issues, but can save stuff like hinges).


local function CallOnChildren(Instance, FunctionToCall)
	-- Calls a function on each of the children of a certain object, using recursion.  

	FunctionToCall(Instance)

	for _, Child in next, Instance:GetChildren() do
		CallOnChildren(Child, FunctionToCall)
	end
end

local function GetNearestParent(Instance, ClassName)
	-- Returns the nearest parent of a certain class, or returns nil

	local Ancestor = Instance
	repeat
		Ancestor = Ancestor.Parent
		if Ancestor == nil then
			return nil
		end
	until Ancestor:IsA(ClassName)

	return Ancestor
end

local function GetBricks(StartInstance)
	local List = {}

	-- if StartInstance:IsA("BasePart") then
	-- 	List[#List+1] = StartInstance
	-- end

	CallOnChildren(StartInstance, function(Item)
		if Item:IsA("BasePart") then
			List[#List+1] = Item;
		end
	end)

	return List
end

local function Modify(Instance, Values)
	-- Modifies an Instance by using a table.  

	assert(type(Values) == "table", "Values is not a table");

	for Index, Value in next, Values do
		if type(Index) == "number" then
			Value.Parent = Instance
		else
			Instance[Index] = Value
		end
	end
	return Instance
end

local function Make(ClassType, Properties)
	-- Using a syntax hack to create a nice way to Make new items.  

	return Modify(Instance.new(ClassType), Properties)
end

local Surfaces = {"TopSurface", "BottomSurface", "LeftSurface", "RightSurface", "FrontSurface", "BackSurface"}
local HingSurfaces = {"Hinge", "Motor", "SteppingMotor"}

local function HasWheelJoint(Part)
	for _, SurfaceName in pairs(Surfaces) do
		for _, HingSurfaceName in pairs(HingSurfaces) do
			if Part[SurfaceName].Name == HingSurfaceName then
				return true
			end
		end
	end
	
	return false
end

local function ShouldBreakJoints(Part)
	--- We do not want to break joints of wheels/hinges. This takes the utmost care to not do this. There are
	--  definitely some edge cases. 

	if NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS then
		return false
	end
	
	if HasWheelJoint(Part) then
		return false
	end
	
	local Connected = Part:GetConnectedParts()
	
	if #Connected == 1 then
		return false
	end
	
	for _, Item in pairs(Connected) do
		if HasWheelJoint(Item) then
			return false
		elseif not Item:IsDescendantOf(script.Parent) then
			return false
		end
	end
	
	return true
end

local function WeldTogether(Part0, Part1, JointType, WeldParent)
	--- Weld's 2 parts together
	-- @param Part0 The first part
	-- @param Part1 The second part (Dependent part most of the time).
	-- @param [JointType] The type of joint. Defaults to weld.
	-- @param [WeldParent] Parent of the weld, Defaults to Part0 (so GC is better).
	-- @return The weld created.

	JointType = JointType or "Weld"
	local RelativeValue = Part1:FindFirstChild("qRelativeCFrameWeldValue")
	
	local NewWeld = Part1:FindFirstChild("qCFrameWeldThingy") or Instance.new(JointType)
	Modify(NewWeld, {
		Name = "qCFrameWeldThingy";
		Part0  = Part0;
		Part1  = Part1;
		C0     = CFrame.new();--Part0.CFrame:inverse();
		C1     = RelativeValue and RelativeValue.Value or Part1.CFrame:toObjectSpace(Part0.CFrame); --Part1.CFrame:inverse() * Part0.CFrame;-- Part1.CFrame:inverse();
		Parent = Part1;
	})

	if not RelativeValue then
		RelativeValue = Make("CFrameValue", {
			Parent     = Part1;
			Name       = "qRelativeCFrameWeldValue";
			Archivable = true;
			Value      = NewWeld.C1;
		})
	end

	return NewWeld
end

local function WeldParts(Parts, MainPart, JointType, DoNotUnanchor)
	-- @param Parts The Parts to weld. Should be anchored to prevent really horrible results.
	-- @param MainPart The part to weld the model to (can be in the model).
	-- @param [JointType] The type of joint. Defaults to weld. 
	-- @parm DoNotUnanchor Boolean, if true, will not unachor the model after cmopletion.
	
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if ShouldBreakJoints(Part) then
			Part:BreakJoints()
		end
	end
	
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if Part ~= MainPart then
			WeldTogether(MainPart, Part, JointType, MainPart)
		end
	end

	if not DoNotUnanchor then
		for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
			Part.Anchored = false
		end
		MainPart.Anchored = false
	end
end

local function PerfectionWeld()	
	local Tool = GetNearestParent(script, "Tool")

	local Parts = GetBricks(script.Parent)
	local PrimaryPart = Tool and Tool:FindFirstChild("Handle") and Tool.Handle:IsA("BasePart") and Tool.Handle or script.Parent:IsA("Model") and script.Parent.PrimaryPart or Parts[1]

	if PrimaryPart then
		WeldParts(Parts, PrimaryPart, "Weld", false)
	else
		warn("qWeld - Unable to weld part")
	end
	
	return Tool
end

local Tool = PerfectionWeld()


if Tool and script.ClassName == "Script" then
	--- Don't bother with local scripts

	script.Parent.AncestryChanged:connect(function()
		PerfectionWeld()
	end)
end
